{com}. 
. * Load the prepared dataset
. use "data/turkey_macro_data.dta", clear
{txt}
{com}. 
. ********************************************************************************
. * 1. Enhanced Data Preparation
. ********************************************************************************
. * Set time series
. tsset year
{res}
{p 0 15 2}{txt:Time variable: }{res:year}{txt:, }{res:{bind:1960}}{txt: to }{res:{bind:2022}}{p_end}
{txt}{col 9}Delta: {res}1 unit
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Generate period dummies for structural breaks
. gen period1 = (year < 1980)        // Pre-liberalization
{txt}
{com}. gen period2 = (year >= 1980 & year < 2001)  // Post-liberalization
{txt}
{com}. gen period3 = (year >= 2001)       // Post-2001 crisis
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Label periods
. label define periods 1 "Pre-liberalization" 2 "Post-liberalization" 3 "Post-2001"
{txt}
{com}. label values period1 periods
{txt}
{com}. label values period2 periods
{txt}
{com}. label values period3 periods
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Generate 3-year moving averages for smoothed analysis
. foreach var of varlist gdp_growth trade_gdp investment inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     gen `var'_ma3 = (l1.`var' + `var' + f1.`var')/3
{txt}  3{com}.     label variable `var'_ma3 "3-year MA of `var'"
{txt}  4{com}. {c )-}
{txt}(3 missing values generated)
(2 missing values generated)
(2 missing values generated)
(2 missing values generated)
(50 missing values generated)
(22 missing values generated)

{com}. 
. ********************************************************************************
. * 2. Descriptive Statistics
. ********************************************************************************
. * Overall summary statistics
. estpost summarize gdp_growth trade_gdp investment inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ, detail

>            (scatter `var' year if year == 2001, mlabel(year) msymbol(D)), ///
>            title("`var' Over Time with Key Events", size(medium)) ///
>            subtitle("With 3-year Moving Average") ///
>            xtitle("Year") ytitle("`var'") ///
>            xline(1980 2001, lpattern(dash) lcolor(gray)) ///
>            legend(order(1 "Actual" 2 "3-year MA" 3 "Liberalization" 4 "2001 Crisis")) ///

. ********************************************************************************
. * 4. Advanced Statistical Analysis
. ********************************************************************************
. * Stationarity tests
. foreach var of varlist gdp_growth trade_gdp investment inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     dfuller `var', trend
{txt}  3{com}. {c )-}

{txt}Dickey–Fuller test for unit root{col 44}Number of obs  = {res}{ralign 2:61}
{txt}Variable: {res}gdp_growth{txt}{col 44}Number of lags = {res}{ralign 2:0}

{txt}H0: Random walk with or without drift

{col 40}Dickey–Fuller
{col 20}Test{col 30}{hline 8} critical value {hline 9}
              statistic           1%           5%          10%
{hline 62}
 Z(t)       {res}     -7.731       -4.126       -3.489       -3.173
{txt}{hline 62}

. ********************************************************************************
. * 7. Improved Marginal Effects Analysis
. ********************************************************************************
. * Load the main dataset and recreate all necessary variables
. use "data/turkey_macro_data.dta", clear
{txt}
{com}. tsset year
{res}
{p 0 15 2}{txt:Time variable: }{res:year}{txt:, }{res:{bind:1960}}{txt: to }{res:{bind:2022}}{p_end}
{txt}{col 9}Delta: {res}1 unit
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Generate period dummies for structural breaks
. gen period1 = (year < 1980)        // Pre-liberalization
{txt}
{com}. gen period2 = (year >= 1980 & year < 2001)  // Post-liberalization
{txt}
{com}. gen period3 = (year >= 2001)       // Post-2001 crisis
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Label periods
. label define periods 1 "Pre-liberalization" 2 "Post-liberalization" 3 "Post-2001"
{txt}
{com}. label values period1 periods
{txt}
{com}. label values period2 periods
{txt}
{com}. label values period3 periods
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Regenerate standardized variables
. foreach var of varlist gdp_growth trade_gdp investment inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     egen std_`var' = std(`var')
{txt}  3{com}.     label variable std_`var' "Standardized `var'"
{txt}  4{com}. {c )-}
{txt}(1 missing value generated)
(48 missing values generated)
(14 missing values generated)

{com}. 
. * Center variables for interaction analysis
. foreach var of varlist trade_gdp investment {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     sum `var'
{txt}  3{com}.     gen c_`var' = `var' - r(mean)
{txt}  4{com}. {c )-}

{txt}    Variable {c |}        Obs        Mean    Std. dev.       Min        Max

. * Generate interaction term explicitly
. gen c_trade_inv_int = c_trade_gdp * c_investment

{com}. 
. * Store coefficients for marginal effects calculation
. local b_trade = _b[c_trade_gdp]
{txt}
{com}. local b_int = _b[c_trade_inv_int]
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Generate range of investment values for marginal effects
. preserve
{txt}
{com}. drop if missing(c_investment)
{txt}(0 observations deleted)

{com}. sum c_investment

{txt}    Variable {c |}        Obs        Mean    Std. dev.       Min        Max
{hline 13}{c +}{hline 57}
c_investment {c |}{res}         63    1.83e-08    4.267646  -9.020441   7.001482
{txt}
{com}. local min_inv = r(min)
{txt}
{com}. local max_inv = r(max)
{txt}
{com}. 
. tempname memhold
{txt}
{com}. postfile `memhold' inv_level marg_effect se_marg using "output/marginal_effects.dta", replace
{txt}
{com}. 
. forvalues inv = -2(0.25)2 {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     * Calculate marginal effect
.     local marg = `b_trade' + `b_int' * `inv'
{txt}  3{com}.     
.     * Calculate standard error of marginal effect
.     lincom c_trade_gdp + `inv' * c_trade_inv_int
{txt}  4{com}.     
.     post `memhold' (`inv') (`marg') (r(se))
{txt}  5{com}. {c )-}

. * Test joint significance of trade variables
. test c_trade_gdp c_trade_inv_int

{p 0 7}{space 1}{text:( 1)}{space 1} {res}c_trade_gdp = 0{p_end}
{p 0 7}{space 1}{text:( 2)}{space 1} c_trade_inv_int = 0{p_end}

{txt}       F(  2,     8) ={res}    0.84
{txt}{col 13}Prob > F ={res}    0.4665
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Calculate standardized coefficients
. quietly sum gdp_growth
{txt}
{com}. local sd_y = r(sd)
{txt}
{com}. foreach var of varlist c_trade_gdp c_investment c_trade_inv_int inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     quietly sum `var'
{txt}  3{com}.     local sd_`var' = r(sd)
{txt}  4{com}.     local b_`var' = _b[`var']
{txt}  5{com}.     local beta_`var' = `b_`var'' * `sd_`var'' / `sd_y'
{txt}  6{com}. {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Display standardized coefficients
. di "Standardized coefficients:"
{res}Standardized coefficients:
{txt}
{com}. foreach var of varlist c_trade_gdp c_investment c_trade_inv_int inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     di "`var': " %6.4f `beta_`var''
{txt}  3{com}. {c )-}
c_trade_gdp: 0.3327
c_investment: -1.3712
c_trade_inv_int: 1.0220
inflation: -1.3699
govt_exp: -0.7516
tertiary_educ: 1.6059
{txt}
{com}. 
. * Export standardized coefficients to file
. file open beta_out using "output/standardized_coefficients.txt", write replace
{txt}
{com}. file write beta_out "Variable,Standardized Coefficient" _n
{txt}
{com}. foreach var of varlist c_trade_gdp c_investment c_trade_inv_int inflation govt_exp tertiary_educ {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.     file write beta_out "`var'," %6.4f (`beta_`var'') _n
{txt}  3{com}. {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. file close beta_out
{txt}

{com}. 
. * Generate confidence intervals
. gen upper_ci = b_trade + 1.96*se_trade
{txt}(15 missing values generated)

{com}. gen lower_ci = b_trade - 1.96*se_trade
{txt}(15 missing values generated)

{com}. 
. * Plot rolling coefficients
. twoway (line b_trade year if !missing(b_trade), lcolor(navy)) ///
>        (line upper_ci year if !missing(upper_ci), lpattern(dash) lcolor(gray)) ///
>        (line lower_ci year if !missing(lower_ci), lpattern(dash) lcolor(gray)), ///
>     title("Rolling Window Estimates: Trade Effect on Growth", size(medium)) ///
>     subtitle("15-year rolling window", size(small)) ///
>     xtitle("End Year of Rolling Window") ytitle("Coefficient Estimate") ///
>     legend(order(1 "Coefficient" 2 "95% CI")) ///
>     note("Note: Dashed lines represent 95% confidence intervals") ///
>     graphregion(color(white)) bgcolor(white) ///
>     saving("output/rolling_coefficients.gph", replace)
{res}{txt}file {bf:output/rolling_coefficients.gph} saved
